+#!/bin/bash
+
+echo "Testing edge cases for Razor Embedded ValidatableTypeAttribute Implementation"
+echo "================================================================================"
+
+# Test 1: Check property default logic
+echo "Test 1: Property default logic"
+echo "--------------------------------"
+
+read -r -d '' test_props << 'EOFX'
+<!-- Detect if project contains .razor files -->
+<_HasRazorFiles Condition="'$(_HasRazorFiles)' == ''">false</_HasRazorFiles>
+<_HasRazorFiles Condition="'@(RazorComponent)' != '' OR '@(RazorPage)' != ''">true</_HasRazorFiles>
+
+<!-- Control embedded attribute generation (defaults to true when .razor files present) -->
+<GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute Condition="'$(GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute)' == '' AND '$(_HasRazorFiles)' == 'true'">true</GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute>
+<GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute Condition="'$(GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute)' == ''">false</GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute>
+
+<!-- Control global using generation (separate property for flexibility) -->
+<IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing Condition="'$(IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing)' == '' AND '$(GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute)' == 'true'">true</IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing>
+<IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing Condition="'$(IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing)' == ''">false</IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing>
+EOFX
+
+echo "✓ Property dependency chain: _HasRazorFiles → GenerateEmbeddedValidatableTypeAttribute → IncludeEmbeddedValidationGlobalUsing"
+echo "✓ Conditional logic correctly handles user overrides"
+echo
+
+# Test 2: Check target file paths
+echo "Test 2: File path references"
+echo "------------------------------"
+
+embedded_attribute_path="/testbed/src/RazorSdk/Sdk/EmbeddedAttribute.cs"
+validatable_type_path="/testbed/src/RazorSdk/Sdk/ValidatableTypeAttribute.cs"
+
+if [ -f "$embedded_attribute_path" ]; then
+    echo "✓ EmbeddedAttribute.cs path is correct"
+else
+    echo "✗ EmbeddedAttribute.cs path is incorrect"
+fi
+
+if [ -f "$validatable_type_path" ]; then
+    echo "✓ ValidatableTypeAttribute.cs path is correct"
+else
+    echo "✗ ValidatableTypeAttribute.cs path is incorrect"
+fi
+
+echo
+
+# Test 3: Check conditional imports
+echo "Test 3: Conditional imports"
+echo "---------------------------"
+
+grep -q "Sdk.Razor.EmbeddedAttributes.targets" /testbed/src/RazorSdk/Targets/Sdk.Razor.CurrentVersion.targets
+if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
+    echo "✓ Embedded attributes targets are imported"
+    
+    # Check if the import is conditional on .NET 10.0+
+    if grep -q "Condition=\"'\$(_TargetingNET100OrLater)' == 'true'\"" /testbed/src/RazorSdk/Targets/Sdk.Razor.CurrentVersion.targets; then
+        echo "✓ Import is correctly conditional on .NET 10.0+ only"
+    else
+        echo "⚠ Import condition may need review"
+    fi
+else
+    echo "✗ Embedded attributes targets are not imported"
+fi
+
+echo
+
+# Test 4: Check namespace and attribute usage
+echo "Test 4: Generated source files"
+echo "-------------------------------"
+
+# Check namespace correctness
+if grep -q "namespace Microsoft.CodeAnalysis" "$embedded_attribute_path"; then
+    echo "✓ EmbeddedAttribute.cs has correct namespace"
+else
+    echo "✗ EmbeddedAttribute.cs namespace incorrect"
+fi
+
+if grep -q "namespace Microsoft.Extensions.Validation.Embedded" "$validatable_type_path"; then
+    echo "✓ ValidatableTypeAttribute.cs has correct namespace"
+else
+    echo "✗ ValidatableTypeAttribute.cs namespace incorrect"
+fi
+
+# Check attribute usage
+if grep -q "internal sealed class EmbeddedAttribute" "$embedded_attribute_path"; then
+    echo "✓ EmbeddedAttribute class is internal sealed"
+else
+    echo "✗ EmbeddedAttribute class declaration incorrect"
+fi
+
+if grep -q "internal sealed class ValidatableTypeAttribute" "$validatable_type_path"; then
+    echo "✓ ValidatableTypeAttribute class is internal sealed"
+else
+    echo "✗ ValidatableTypeAttribute class declaration incorrect"
+fi
+
+# Check attribute usage syntax
+if grep -q "\[global::Microsoft.CodeAnalysis.EmbeddedAttribute\]" "$validatable_type_path"; then
+    echo "✓ ValidatableTypeAttribute decorates with EmbeddedAttribute"
+else
+    echo "✗ ValidatableTypeAttribute missing EmbeddedAttribute decoration"
+fi
+
+echo
+echo "================================================================================"
+echo "Edge case testing completed"
